   Ṛgveda 8	Ṛgveda 8
   RV_8,001.01a mā cid anyad vi śaṃsata sakhāyo mā riṣaṇyata |	RV_8,001.01a mA cit anyat vi SaMsata saKAyaH mA rizaNyate |
   RV_8,001.01c indram it stotā vṛṣaṇaṃ sacā sute muhur ukthā ca śaṃsata ||	RV_8,001.01t indram id stotA vRzaNam sacA sute muhur ukTA ca SaMsate ||
   RV_8,001.02a avakrakṣiṇaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ yathājuraṃ gāṃ na carṣaṇīsaham |	RV_8,001.02a avakrakziNam vRzaBam yaTA-Ajuram gAm na ca-RzaNI-saham |
   RV_8,001.02c vidveṣaṇaṃ saṃvananobhayaṅkaram maṃhiṣṭham ubhayāvinam ||	RV_8,001.02t vidvezaNam saMvanana-uBayaFkaram maMhizWam uBayAvinam ||
